$(document).ready(function(){
  var isMobile = {
    Android: function() {
        return navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i);
    },
    BlackBerry: function() {
        return navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i);
    },
    iOS: function() {
        return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone|iPad|iPod/i);
    },
    Opera: function() {
        return navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera Mini/i);
    },
    Windows: function() {
        return navigator.userAgent.match(/IEMobile/i);
    },
    any: function() {
        return (isMobile.Android() || isMobile.BlackBerry() || isMobile.iOS() || isMobile.Opera() || isMobile.Windows());
    }
};
if(!isMobile.any()) {


var script = document.createElement('script');
script.src = "js/ZeroClipboard.js";
document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0].parentNode.appendChild(script);

var script = document.createElement('script');
script.src = "js/mootools.1.2.3.js";
document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0].parentNode.appendChild(script);
  copyclipboard();
   //alert("This is a not Mobile Device");

}
else{
  //alert('This is a mobile device');
}

});

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function delete_text(){
  $('#InputText').val(null);
  document.getElementById('TranslationOutput').textContent="";
  $("#count_word").html(0);
  $("#count_character").html(0);
}

function trim(str)
{
return str.replace(/^\s*|\s*$/g,"");
}
function download_TTS(vt,language, from_translated){
    if(vt==""){
        alert("Please type your text firstly.");
        return false;
    }
	if(vt.length > 1000){
        alert("Too many characters for one request!");
        return false;
    }
	var link = window.location.href.split("/");
	link.pop();
	link = link.join("/")+'/audio.php';
	var form = document.createElement("form");
		form.setAttribute("method", 'post');
		form.setAttribute("action", link);
	var hiddenField = document.createElement("input");
		hiddenField.setAttribute("type", "hidden");
		hiddenField.setAttribute("name", 'word');
		hiddenField.setAttribute("value", vt);
	form.appendChild(hiddenField);
	if(!from_translated){
		language = language_code(language);
	}
	if(language != ''){
		hiddenField = document.createElement("input");
		hiddenField.setAttribute("type", "hidden");
		hiddenField.setAttribute("name", 'lang');
		hiddenField.setAttribute("value", language);
		form.appendChild(hiddenField);
	}
	document.body.appendChild(form);
    form.submit();
	// window.location.replace(link);
}
function audio1_input()
{
   var j;
  var i;
  text=document.getElementsByName('InputText').item(0).value;
  text12=document.getElementById("__LangPair_FromDDL_header").innerHTML;
  text1=trim(text12);
	text1 = language_code(text1);
	if(text1 == ''){
		text1 = 'en';
	}


  audio_input(text,text1);

}
function language_code(text1){
	if(text1=="Auto-Detect")
  {

    text1='';
  }
  else if(text1=="Arabic")
  {
    text1='ar';
  }
 else if(text1=="Bulgarian")
  {

    text1="bg";
  }
   else if(text1=="Catalan")
  {
    text1='ca';
  }
  else if(text1=="Chinese Simplified")
  {
    text1='zh-chs';
  }
  else if(text1=="Chinese Traditional")
  {
    text1='zh-cht';
  }
  else if(text1=="Czech")
  {
    text1='cs';
  }
  else if(text1=="Danish")
  {
    text1='da';
  }
  else if(text1=="Dutch")
  {
    text1='nl';
  }
  else if(text1=="English")
  {
    text1='en';
  }
  else if(text1=="Estonian")
  {
    text1='et';
  }
  else if(text1=="Finnish")
  {
    text1='fi';
  }
  else if(text1=="Arabic")
  {
    text1='ar';
  }
  else if(text1=="French")
  {
    text1='fr';
  }
  else if(text1=="Croatian")
  {
    text1='hr';
  }
  else if(text1=="Welsh")
  {
    text1='cy';
  }
  else if(text1=="German")
  {
    text1='de';
  }
  else if(text1=="Greek")
  {
    text1='el';
  }
  else if(text1=="Haitian Creole")
  {
    text1='ht';
  }
  else if(text1=="Hebrew")
  {
    text1='he';
  }
   else if(text1=="Hindi")
  {
    text1='hi';
  }
  else if(text1=="Hungarian")
  {
    text1='hu';
  }
  else if(text1=="Indonesian")
  {
    text1='id';
  }
  else if(text1=="Italian")
  {
    text1='it';
  }
  else if(text1=="Japanese")
  {
    text1='ja';
  }
  else if(text1=="Korean")
  {
    text1='ko';
  }
  else if(text1=="Latvian")
  {
    text1='lv';
  }
  else if(text1=="Lithuanian")
  {
    text1='lt';
  }
  else if(text1=="Norwegian")
  {
    text1='no';
  }
  else if(text1=="Polish")
  {
    text1='pl';
  }
  else if(text1=="Portuguese")
  {
    text1='pt';
  }
  else if(text1=="Romanian")
  {
    text1='ro';
  }
  else if(text1=="Russian")
  {
    text1='ru';
  }
  else if(text1=="Slovak")
  {
    text1='sk';
  }
  else if(text1=="Slovenian")
  {
    text1='sl';
  }
  else if(text1=="Spanish")
  {
    text1='es';
  }
  else if(text1=="Swedish")
  {
    text1='sv';
  }
  else if(text1=="Thai")
  {
    text1='th';
  }
  else if(text1=="Turkish")
  {
    text1="tr";
  }
  else if(text1=="Ukrainian")
  {
    text1='uk';
  }
  else if(text1=="Vietnamese")
  {
    text1='vi';
  }
  else
	{
	  text1="en";
	}
return text1;
}

function audio1_output()
{

  text2=document.getElementById('TranslationOutput').textContent;
  text3=document.getElementsByName('LangPair_ToDDL_svid').item(0).value;


  audio_output(text2,text3);

}

function translate_input()
{

Default.RtlLanguages = 'ar,he';

                 T2S.Init('A16F6A4B41D5113A8DBC25E2320906FC2C0E87C8',true,450,'https://api.microsofttranslator.com/V2/Http.svc');
                 Default.Service.Dictionary.IsActive = true;
                 Default.Service.Dictionary.SupportedLP = 'ko-en,en-ko,ja-en,en-ja,zh-en,en-zh,es-en,en-es,it-en,en-it,de-en,en-de,fr-en,en-fr';
                 Default.Service.Dictionary.MaxWords = 4;
                 Default.Service.Dictionary.MaxOverride = 'de:1,en:1,es:1,fr:1,it:1';
                 Default.UI.SupportedTTSLanguages = 'ca,ca-es,da,da-dk,de,de-de,en,en-au,en-ca,en-gb,en-in,en-us,es,es-es,es-mx,fi,fi-fi,fr,fr-ca,fr-fr,it,it-it,ja,ja-jp,ko,ko-kr,nb-no,nl,nl-nl,no,pl,pl-pl,pt,pt-br,pt-pt,ru,ru-ru,sv,sv-se,zh-chs,zh-cht,zh-cn,zh-hk,zh-tw';

  Default.Service.Translate();
    var characters = $("#InputText").val();
    var count_characters =characters.length;
    $("#count_character").html(count_characters);
    var words = $('#InputText').val().split(' ');
    var count_words=words.length;
    $("#count_word").html(count_words);
}

<div class="about-content">
<p>Our webpage offers online free translation services for numerous languages. We have a basic online language translator that is machine-based that helps the user undertake <strong>free translation</strong> of any word, phrase, or sentence they may want to. This free online translator, however, is not fully accurate. It manages to convey a basic idea and sense of what was meant in the original language, but it cannot convey the fine nuances of the text. For that, we offer you best <strong>professional translation services</strong>. These are done by experts in the languages concerned who can provide you with a professional language translation of your documents. For a quote, you can submit your documents through our <strong>document translation</strong> page. We can assure you the end result of our professional translation and proofreading services will be both free of errors and reasonably priced for your budget. </p>

<td class="mttextareainit" id="InstText" style="color: #000; font-family: Tahoma, Geneva, sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-size:13px;"><a href="https://aka.ms/MicrosoftTranslatorAttribution" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" style="float:right"><img src="images/free-translation.jpg" /></a></td>

<div style="background: #136b9a;color: #fff;width: 100%;padding: 8px;font-size: 19px;text-align: center;font-weight: bold;"><h2>Document Translation Services</h2></div>
</div>
<div class="col-md-12">
<div style="float:left;width: 100%;height: auto;padding: 10px;background: #e4e4e4;font-size: 15px;text-align: justify;
">
<img src="images/professional-translation-services.jpg" alt="professional translation services" width="350px" style="float: left;margin-right: 10px;" />
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">We at Transfree have created a niche for ourselves in the field of free and professional translation services. Unlike other free translators, it supports 51 languages to translate, convert text to speech and download audio of texts.<p>
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">Our translation agency has native professional translators and proofreaders on board who are adept at translating and proofreading while keeping the nuances of the language in mind. They have, without exception, significant knowledge of their native languages as well as the languages they translate to. The translations are done keeping in mind the cultural sensitivities of both of the languages concerned.<p>
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">Besides being experts in the languages concerned, the translators on our panel are also experts in various subjects. Your document could be in any subject; be it sociology, physics, astronomy, economics, law, medicine, engineering or history. Our professional translators and proofreaders are bound to give you satisfactory results. So whatever the subject of the document that you need to get translated or proofread, you can be certain that the end product will be of uniformly high quality and free of errors.<p>
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">We also assure you of timely turnaround with the quality of language translation and proofreading services we offer, so there need be no worry about the finished product in any way, be it content or time taken or the accuracy therein. We understand how important it is for our clients to get their translation work delivered in time and we are, therefore, mindful of meeting deadlines our customers set for us.<p>
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">Our area of expertise for professional translation and proofreading services include brochures, manuals, project reports, books, birth records, contracts and any other projects. Besides these, we also undertake academic articles and theses that we assure of being competently translated and proofread from the source language to the target language. The translated work is also edited and proofread by our staff so the final document that you get in hand is sure to be of an uncompromising quality and with no mistakes.<p>
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">The range of professional document translation and proofreading services we offer are presented in the list ahead:</p>
<ul style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;list-style: circle;list-style: circle;list-style-type: circle;padding-left: 16px; padding-top: 10px;">
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Business translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Financial translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Legal translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Literary translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Medical translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Academic translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Technical translation services</li>
<li style="list-style-type:circle">Website translation services</li><br>
<p style="font-size: 14px;line-height: 1.6;text-align: justify;">As Transfree translation agency, we offer all the benefits mentioned above at a price that is competitive with most other translation agencies in the industry. We assure you that once you have availed of our professional translation and proofreading services meeting your deadlines at reasonable costs, you will always stay with us.</p>

              function copyclipboard(){
             //window.addEvent("load",function() {
      setTimeout(function() {
        //set path
        ZeroClipboard.setMoviePath('js/ZeroClipboard.swf');
        //create client
        var clip = new ZeroClipboard.Client();
        //event
        clip.addEventListener('mousedown',function() {

          clip.setText(document.getElementById('TranslationOutput').innerText);
        });
        clip.addEventListener('complete',function(client,text) {
          $( "#copy23" ).hide().delay(1100).fadeIn();
          $("#loader").show().delay(500).fadeOut();
        //alert('copied: ' + text);
         });
        //glue it to the button
        clip.glue('copy23');
      }, 2000);
      }
